function cmp (a, b) {
let pa = a.split('.');
let pb = b.split('.');
for (let i = 0; i &lt; Math.max(pa.length, pb.length); i++) {
let na = Number(pa[i]);
let nb = Number(pb[i]);
if (isNaN(na)) na = 0;
if (isNaN(nb)) nb = 0;
if (na &gt; nb) return "Older";
if (nb &gt; na) return "Newer";
}
return "Same";
};
